# <a name="essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-103">Office būtiskie pakalpojumi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-103">Essential services for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-104">Informācija šajā rakstā attiecas uz tālāk minētās Office klienta programmatūras versiju 1904 vai jaunāku versiju, kas instalēta datorā, kurā darbojas sistēma Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-105">Office 365 ProPlus un Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-106">Office 365 individuālai lietošanai, Office 365 mājas lietošanai vai citas Office versijas, kas ir daļa no Office 365 abonementa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-107">Project un Visio, kas ir iekļautas dažos abonēšanas plānos, piemēram, Project Online Professional plānā vai Visio Online 2. plānā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-108">Office sastāv no klienta programmām un saistītajiem līdzekļiem, kas paredzēti, lai jūs varētu efektīvāk veidot, sazināties un sadarboties.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-108">Office consists of client software applications and connected experiences designed to enable you to create, communicate, and collaborate more effectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-109">Lai gan varat kontrolēt daudzas savienotās iespējas, kas ir pieejamas jums vai jūsu lietotājiem, ja esat savas organizācijas administrators, pastāv pakalpojumu kopa, kas ir būtiski attiecībā uz to, kā Office darbojas, tāpēc tos nevar atspējot.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-109">While you can control many of the connected experiences that are available to you, or to your users if you’re the admin in your organization, there are a set of services that are essential to how Office functions and therefore cannot be disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-110">Piemēram, licencēšanas pakalpojums, kas apstiprina, vai esat pareizi licencēts Office izmantošanai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-110">For example, the licensing service that confirms that you are properly licensed to use Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-111">Nepieciešamie pakalpojumu dati par šiem pakalpojumiem tiek apkopoti un nosūtīti korporācijai Microsoft neatkarīgi no citiem politikas iestatījumiem, kas saistīti ar konfidencialitāti un kurus esat konfigurējis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-111">Required service data about these services is collected and sent to Microsoft, regardless of any other privacy-related policy settings that you have configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-112">Šos datus varat skatīt, izmantojot diagnostikas datu skatītāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-112">You can see this data by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-113">Papildinformāciju skatiet šeit:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-113">For more information, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-114">Office nepieciešamais datu pakalpojums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-114">Required service data for Office</span></span>](required-service-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-115">Diagnostikas datu skatītāja izmantošana ar Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-115">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-116">Office saistītie līdzekļi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-116">Connected experiences in Office</span></span>](connected-experiences.md)

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-117">Ja esat organizācijas administrators, iespējams, jūs interesēs arī šie raksti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-117">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-118">Pārskats par konfidencialitātes kontroles līdzekļiem pakalpojumā Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-118">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-119">Politikas iestatījumu izmantošana Office 365 ProPlus konfidencialitātes kontroles pārvaldībai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-119">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="list-of-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-120">Office būtisko pakalpojumu saraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-120">List of essential services for Office</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-121">Tālāk esošajā tabulā ir Office būtisko pakalpojumu saraksts, kā arī katra pakalpojuma apraksts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-121">The following table provides a list of the essential services for Office and a description of each service.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-122">**Pakalpojums**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-122">**Service**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-123">**Apraksts**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-123">**Description**</span></span>  |
| ------ | ---- |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-124">Autentifikācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-124">Authentication</span></span>](#authentication-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-125">Autentifikācija ir vairāku platformu pakalpojums, kas pārbauda jūsu Office lietotāja identitāti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-125">Authentication is a cross-platform service that validates your Office user identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-126"> Tā ir nepieciešama, lai jums sniegtu iespēju pierakstīties sistēmā Office, aktivizēt jūsu Office licenci, piekļūtu jūsu mākonī saglabātajiem failiem, kā arī nodrošinātu konsekventu pieredzi vairākās Office sesijās un jūsu ierīcēs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-126"> It is required to enable you to sign in to Office, activate your Office license, access your files stored in the cloud, and provides a consistent experience across Office sessions and your devices.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-127">Click-to-Run</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-127">Click-to-Run</span></span>](#click-to-run-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-128">Click-to-Run ir instalēšanas tehnoloģija, kas tiek izmantota, lai instalētu un atjauninātu sistēmu Office operētājsistēmā Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-128">Click-to-Run is the installation technology used to install and update Office on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-129">Tā meklē jaunas Office versijas un, kad jauna versija ir pieejama, lejupielādē un instalē to.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-129">It checks for new versions of Office, and when a new version is available, downloads and installs it.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-130"> Click-to-Run noteiks Office atjauninājumu (tostarp drošības atjauninājumu) nepieciešamību, veiks to lejupielādi un instalēšanu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-130"> Click-to-Run will detect the need for, perform the download of, and install Office updates, including security updates.</span></span>     |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-131">Uzlabotās konfigurācijas pakalpojums (ECS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-131">Enhanced Configuration Service (ECS)</span></span>](#enhanced-configuration-service-ecs-events) | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-132">ECS nodrošina korporācijai Microsoft iespēju atkārtoti konfigurēt Office instalācijas tā, lai jums nebūtu atkārtoti jāizvieto Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-132">ECS provides Microsoft the ability to reconfigure Office installations without the need for you to redeploy Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-133">Tā tiek izmantota, lai kontrolētu pakāpenisko līdzekļu vai atjauninājumu ieviešanu, kamēr ieviešanas ietekme tiek pārraudzīta no diagnostikas datiem, kas tiek apkopoti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-133">It is used to control the gradual rollout of features or updates, while the impact of the rollout is monitored from diagnostic data being collected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-134">Tā arī tiek izmantota, lai mazinātu drošības vai veiktspējas problēmas ar līdzekli vai atjauninājumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-134">It is also used to mitigate security or performance issues with a feature or update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-135">Turklāt ECS atbalsta konfigurācijas izmaiņas, kas saistītas ar diagnostikas datiem, lai nodrošinātu, ka tiek apkopoti atbilstošie notikumi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-135">In addition, ECS supports configuration changes related to diagnostic data to help ensure that the appropriate events are being collected.</span></span> |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-136">Licencēšana</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-136">Licensing</span></span>](#licensing-events)     | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-137">Licencēšana ir mākoņpakalpojums, kas atbalsta jūsu Office aktivizāciju jaunām instalācijām, kā arī uztur licenci jūsu ierīcēs pēc Office aktivizēšanas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-137">Licensing is a cloud-based service that supports your Office activation for new installations and maintains the license on your devices after Office has been activated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-138">Tā reģistrē katru jūsu ierīci un aktivizē Office, pārbauda jūsu Office abonementa statusu un pārvalda jūsu produktu atslēgas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-138">It registers each of your devices and activates Office, checks the status of your Office subscription, and manages your product keys.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-139">Pakalpojumu konfigurācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-139">Services Configuration</span></span>](#services-configuration-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-140">Pakalpojumu konfigurācija nodrošina iespēju veikt atjauninājumus Office konfigurācijas iestatījumos, lai iespējotu vai atspējotu klientu līdzekļus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-140">Services Configuration provides the ability to make updates to Office configuration settings to enable or disable client features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-141">Tā tiek izsaukta ikreiz, kad Office lietojumprogramma tiek startēta, un nodrošina detalizētu informāciju par citām Office konfigurācijām un pakalpojumiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-141">It is called every time an Office application is started and provides details about other Office configurations and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-142">Pakalpojumu konfigurācija kontrolē arī to, kuri pakalpojumi ir paredzēti kā būtiskie pakalpojumi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-142">Services Configuration also controls which services are designated as essential services.</span></span>  |
| [<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-143">Telemetrijas dati </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-143">Telemetry </span></span>](#telemetry-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-144">Telemetrijas datu pakalpojums tiek izmantots, lai apkopotu diagnostikas datus no Office lietojumprogrammām.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-144">The Telemetry service is used to collect diagnostic data from Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-145">Tas nodrošina Office ģenerēto diagnostikas datu apkopošanu — gan obligāto, gan papildu diagnostikas datu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-145">It enables the collection of the diagnostic data generated by Office, both required and optional diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-146">Tas ir arī atbildīgs par Office nepieciešamo pakalpojuma datu pakalpojuma diagnostikas datu daļas apkopošanu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-146">It is also responsible for the collection of the service diagnostic data portion of required service data for Office.</span></span>  |

## <a name="events-and-data-fields-for-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-147">Office būtisko pakalpojumu notikumu un datu lauki</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-147">Events and data fields for essential services for Office</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-148">Nākamajās sadaļās ir sniegta tālāk norādītā informācija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-148">The next sections provide the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-149">Notikumu saraksts katram būtiskajam pakalpojumam</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-149">A list of events for each essential service</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-150">Katra notikuma apraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-150">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-151">Datu lauku saraksts katrā notikumā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-151">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-152">Katra datu lauka apraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-152">A description of each data field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-153">Šos notikumus varat skatīt, izmantojot diagnostikas datu skatītāju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-153">You can see these events by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>



## <a name="authentication-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-154">Autentifikācijas notikumi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-154">Authentication events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-155">Šie diagnostikas datu notikumi tiek apkopoti, kad Office mēģina iegūt autentifikācijas marķieri vai nu nemanāmi vai izmantojot uzvedni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-155">These diagnostic data events are collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentityfbapromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-157">Tiek apkopots, kad Office rāda lietotājam uz veidlapām balstītas pierakstīšanās uzvedni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-157">Collected when Office shows the user a Forms-Based-Auth sign-in prompt.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-158">Kopā ar kluso pilnvaru iegūšanu autentifikācijas uzvednes tiek izmantotas, lai noteiktu, vai lietotājs ir bojātā autentifikācijas stāvoklī, kas lietotājam izraisa būtībā bezsaistes klienta stāvokli, vai sliktākajā gadījumā bojāta autentifikācija var traucēt licences iegūšanu, kā arī izraisīt pilnībā nelietojamu klientu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-158">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts is used to determine if user is in a broken authentication state which, for the user, results in what is essentially an Offline Client state, or in the worst case, broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-159">Uz veidlapām balstītās autentifikācijas (FBA) pierakstīšanās uzvednes tiek izmantotas dažiem lokāliem autentifikācijas scenārijiem, un parasti mēs vēlamies nodrošināt, ka tā nenotiek, jo visiem vajadzētu lietot moderno autentifikāciju ar FBA saistīto drošības ievainojamību dēļ.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-159">Forms-Based-Auth (FBA) sign-in prompts are used for some on-premises authentication scenarios and typically we want to make sure this isn’t happening, as everyone should be using Modern-Auth because of security vulnerabilities associated with FBA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-160">**Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-160">**The following fields are collected:**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-161">**AuthScheme** — izmantotā autentifikācijas shēma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-161">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-162">**DocumentUrlHash** — šifrēta URL pieprasīšana</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - an encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-163">**EndTag** — tags, kur FBA veidlapa tiek aizpildīta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-163">**EndTag** - the tag where FBA form is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-164">**Flags** — novecojis</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-164">**Flags** - Obsolete</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-165">**FlowTag** — tags, kur FBA veidlapa tiek startēta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-165">**FlowTag** - the tag where FBA form is started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-166">**LastError** — atgrieztais kļūdas kods</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-166">**LastError** – the error code returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-167">**PromptEndTime** — laiks, kad uzvedne tika beigta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-167">**PromptEndTime** - the time when then prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-168">**PromptStartTime** — laiks, kad uzvedne tiek sākta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-168">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-169">**Result** — vai autentifikācija izdevās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-169">**Result** - whether the authentication succeeded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-170">**SessionEndTime** — laiks, kad notikuma sesija beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-170">**SessionEndTime** – the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-171">**Timeout** — laiks, kad uzvednei iestājās taimauts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-171">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt timed out</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysignoutevent"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-173">Tiek apkopots, kad lietotājs izrakstās no Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-173">Collected when a user signs out of Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-174">Zinot, ka lietotājs ir izrakstījies, kļūst iespējams klasificēt citus notikumus, piemēram, uzvednes, kā paredzēts, lai šos notikumus varētu pareizi skaitļot uzticamības/gatavības nosūtīšanai metrikā, kā arī izvairīties no brīdinājumiem vai būvējumu atrites kļūdainā iekārtā, kur lietotājam rodas neparedzētas pierakstīšanās uzvednes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-174">Knowing the user is signed-out makes it possible to classify other events, such as prompts, as expected, so those events can be correctly computed in reliability / ship-readiness metrics and avoid alerting or rolling back builds on the faulty premise that the user is experiencing unexpected sign-in prompts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-175">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-175">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-176">**FlowEndTime** — laiks, kad izrakstīšanās darbība beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-176">**FlowEndTime** - the time when the sign out action ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-177">**FlowStartTime** — laiks, kad izrakstīšanās darbība sākās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-177">**FlowStartTime** - the time when the sign out action started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-178">**IdentityErrorState** — jebkāds identitātes kļūdas stāvoklis izrakstīšanās laikā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-178">**IdentityErrorState** - any identity error state during sign out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** — šifrētais identitātes ID, kam tiek veikta izrakstīšanās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - the encrypted identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-180">**IdentityProviderType** — tās identitātes nodrošinātājs, kurai tiek veikta izrakstīšanās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-180">**IdentityProviderType** - the identity provider of the identity being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-181">**IdentityUniqueID** — identitātes ID, kam tiek veikta izrakstīšanās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - the identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-182">**SessionEndTime** — laiks, kad notikuma sesija beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-182">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-183">**SignOutUserAction** — norāda, ka lietotājs sāk izrakstīšanās darbību</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-183">**SignOutUserAction** - Indicates the user initiates the sign out action</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysspipromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-185">Tiek apkopots, kad Office rāda lietotājam Windows SSPI pierakstīšanās uzvedni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-185">Collected when Office shows the user a Windows SSPI sign-in prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-186">Kopā ar kluso pilnvaru iegūšanu autentifikācijas uzvednes nosaka, vai lietotājs ir bojātā autentifikācijas stāvoklī, kas izraisa bezsaistes klienta stāvokli.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-186">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts determine whether a user is in a broken authentication state, which results in an Offline Client state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-187">Bojāta autentifikācija var traucēt licences iegūšanu, kā arī izraisīt pilnībā nelietojamu klientu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-187">Broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-188">Windows SSPI uzvednes tiek izmantotas autentifikācijai ar Exchange (pasta sinhronizēšanai), ja lietotāja Exchange resurss nav iestatīts daudzfaktoru autentifikācijai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-188">Windows SSPI prompts are used for authenticating with Exchange (for mail synchronizing) when the user's Exchange resource hasn't been setup for multi-factor authentication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-189">Šie notikumi kopā ar Office.MATS nosaukumvietas notikumiem tiek izmantoti tālāk norādītajiem mērķiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-189">These events, along with the Office.MATS namespace events, are used for the following purposes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-190">1.\) Identificēt, vai klienti var sekmīgi iegūt autentifikācijas marķieri vai ir pārgājuši bojātā autentifikācijas stāvoklī.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-190">1\) Identify whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-191">2.\) Novērtēt, vai izmaiņas, kas radušās klientā vai pakalpojumos, ir izraisījušas kritisku regresiju lietotāja autentifikācijas pieredzē un uzticamībā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-191">2\) Evaluate whether changes that have occurred on the client or services have resulted in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-192">3.\) Ja rodas kļūme, šie signāli raida svarīgus kļūmju kodus no atbildīgā komponenta (Office klienta kods, autentifikācijas bibliotēkas vai iestāžu pakalpojumi), ko var izmantot klasificēšanai, diagnostikai un mazināšanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-192">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-193">4.\) Šie signāli nodrošina dažādus nosūtīšanas gatavības un darbspējas pārraugus, kas aktivizē brīdinājumus,lai mūsu inženieri varētu ātri iesaistīties un samazināt laiku kritisko lietotāju bloķēšanas kļūmju mazināšanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-193">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical user-blocking failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-194">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-194">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-195">**AllowSavedCreds** — vai jaunie akreditācijas dati ir pastāvīgi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-195">**AllowSavedCreds** - whether the new credential is persisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-196">**AuthScheme** — izmantotā autentifikācijas shēma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-196">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-197">**CredsSaved** — vai jaunie akreditācijas dati ir saglabāti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-197">**CredsSaved** - whether the new credential is saved</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-198">**DocumentUrlHash** — šifrētā URL pieprasīšana</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-198">**DocumentUrlHash** - the encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-199">**EndTag** — tags, kur uzvedne beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-199">**EndTag** - the tag where the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-200">**NewIdentity**\_ErrorState — vai jaunā identitāte ir derīga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-200">**NewIdentity**\_ErrorState – whether the new identity is valid</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-201">**NewIdentity\_HashedUniqueId** — šifrētais jaunais identitātes ID pēc uzvednes pabeigšanas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-201">**NewIdentity\_HashedUniqueId** - the encrypted new identity ID after prompt is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-203">**NewIdentity\_UniqueID** — jaunais identitātes ID pēc uzvednes pabeigšanas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-203">**NewIdentity\_UniqueID** - the new identity ID after the prompt is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-204">**OutStatus** — vai uzvednes izvade ir derīga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-204">**OutStatus** - whether the prompt output is valid</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-205">**PromptEndTime** — laiks, kad uzvedne tika beigta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-205">**PromptEndTime** - the time when the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-206">**PromptFailedTag** — tags, kas norāda SSPI uzvednes kļūmi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-206">**PromptFailedTag** - the tag that indicates SSPI prompt failure</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-207">**PromptFlow** — tags, kas izsauca SSPI uzvedni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-207">**PromptFlow** - the tag that invoked the SSPI prompt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-208">**PromptStartTime** — laiks, kad uzvedne tiek sākta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-208">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-209">**Proxy** — vai tiek izmantots starpniekserveris</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-209">**Proxy** - if proxy is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-210">**ServerHash** — šifrētā servera adrese</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-210">**ServerHash** - the encrypted server address</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-211">**SessionEndTime** — laiks, kad notikuma sesija beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-211">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

### <a name="officematsactionofficewin32-officematsactionofficewinrt"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-245">Tālāk norādītais apraksts attiecas gan uz Win32, gan WinRT notikumiem (nosaukums ir atkarīgs no platformas).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-245">The following description applies for both Win32 and WinRT events (the name depends on platform.)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-246">Microsoft autentifikācijas telemetrijas sistēma (MATS) tiek apkopota, kad Office mēģina iegūt autentifikācijas marķieri vai nu nemanāmi vai izmantojot uzvedni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) is collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-247">Ja iegūšanas mēģinājumi neizdodas, tiek iekļauta kļūdas informācija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-247">When acquisition attempts fail, error information is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-248">Šie notikumi mūsu lietotājiem sniedz iespēju izvairīties no pāriešanas bojātos autentifikācijas stāvokļos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-248">These events help our users avoid entering broken authentication states by:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-249">1.\) Identificēšana, vai klienti var sekmīgi iegūt autentifikācijas marķieri vai ir pārgājuši bojātā autentifikācijas stāvoklī.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-249">1\) Identifying whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-250">2.\) Novērtēt, kad izmaiņas rodas klientā vai pakalpojumos, vai tās izraisa kritisku regresiju lietotāja autentifikācijas pieredzē un uzticamībā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-250">2\) Evaluate when changes occur on the client or services, whether they result in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-251">3.\) Ja rodas kļūme, šie signāli raida svarīgus kļūmju kodus no atbildīgā komponenta (Office klienta kods, autentifikācijas bibliotēkas vai iestāžu pakalpojumi), ko var izmantot klasificēšanai, diagnostikai un mazināšanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-251">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-252">4.\) Šie signāli nodrošina dažādus nosūtīšanas gatavības un darbspējas pārraugus, kas aktivizē brīdinājumus,lai mūsu inženieri varētu ātri iesaistīties un samazināt laiku kritisko kļūmju mazināšanai.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-252">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-253">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-253">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-254">**Actiontype** — kura autentifikācijas bibliotēka tiek izmantota</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-254">**Actiontype** - Which authentication library is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-255">**Appaudience** — vai lietojumprogrammas būvējums ir paredzēts iekšējai vai ārējai lietošanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-255">**Appaudience** - Is the app build for internal or external use</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-256">**Appforcedprompt** — vai lietojumprogramma ignorēja kešatmiņu un nodrošināja uzvednes rādīšanu piespiedu kārtā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-256">**Appforcedprompt** - Did the app override cache and force a prompt to be shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-257">**Appname** — tās lietojumprogrammas nosaukums, kas veic autentifikāciju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-257">**Appname** - Name of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-258">**Appver** — tās lietojumprogrammas versija, kas veic autentifikāciju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-258">**Appver** - Version of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-259">**Askedforcreds** — vai lietojumprogramma pieprasīja lietotājam ievadīt akreditācijas datus šai darbībai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-259">**Askedforcreds** - Did the application ask the user to enter credentials for this action</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-260">**Authoutcome** — vai autentifikācijas mēģinājums izdevās, neizdevās vai tika atcelts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-260">**Authoutcome** - Did the authentication attempt succeed, fail, or was cancelled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-261">**Blockingprompt** — vai lietojumprogramma parādīja uzvedni, kur bija nepieciešama lietotāja mijiedarbība</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-261">**Blockingprompt** - Did the application throw a prompt requiring user interaction</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-262">**Correlationid** — GUID, kas tiek izmantots savienošanai ar pakalpojumu datiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-262">**Correlationid** - GUID used for joining with services data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-263">**Count** — notikumu skaits apkopojuma gadījumos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-263">**Count** - Count of events in cases of aggregation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-264">**Data\_accounttype** — patērētāja vai organizācijas konts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-264">**Data\_accounttype** - Consumer or organizational account</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-265">**Devicenetworkstate** — vai lietotājs bija tiešsaistē</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-265">**Devicenetworkstate** - Was the user online</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-266">**Deviceprofiletelemetryid** — anonīmais ierīces ID, kas tika izmantots, lai mērītu ierīces pieredzi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-266">**Deviceprofiletelemetryid** - Anonymous device ID used to measure device experience</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-267">**Duration** — cik ilga bija autentifikācija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-267">**Duration** - How long the authentication took</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-268">**Endtime** — kad autentifikācijas notikums beidzās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-268">**Endtime** - When the authentication event ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-269">**Error** — kļūdas kods, ja autentifikācija neizdevās</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-269">**Error** - Error code if the authentication failed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-270">**Errordescription** — īss kļūdas apraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-270">**Errordescription** - Brief description of the error</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-271">**Errorsource** — vai kļūda radās pakalpojumā, autentifikācijas bibliotēkā vai lietojumprogrammā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-271">**Errorsource** - Did the error come from service, authentication library, or application</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-272">**Identityservice** — vai tika izsaukts Microsoft pakalpojuma konts (MSA) vai Azure Active Directory (AAD) pakalpojums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-272">**Identityservice** - Was Microsoft Service Account (MSA) or Azure Active Directory (AAD) service invoked</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-273">**Interactiveauthcontainer** — kāda veida uzvedne tika rādīta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-273">**Interactiveauthcontainer** - What type of prompt was shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-274">**Issilent** — vai uzvedne tika rādīta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-274">**Issilent** - Was a prompt shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-275">**Microsoft**\_**ADAL**\_**adal**\_**version** — Azure Active Directory Authentication Library (ADAL) versija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-275">**Microsoft**\_**ADAL**\_**adal**\_**version** - Version of the Azure Active Directory Authentication Library (ADAL)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-276">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_api\_error\_code** — kļūdas kods, ko raidīja autentifikācijas bibliotēka šim autentifikācijas mēģinājumam</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-276">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_api\_error\_code** - Error code emitted by authentication library for this authentication attempt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-277">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_api\_id** — šim autentifikācijas mēģinājumam izsauktais API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-277">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_api\_id** - API invoked for this authentication attempt</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-278">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority** — Azure Active Directory tās iestādes URL, kas atbildīga par lietotāja autentifikāciju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-278">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority** – Azure Active Directory authority URL responsible for authenticating the user</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-279">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority\_type** — patērētāja/Microsoft pakalpojuma līgums (MSA) attiecībā pret organizāciju/Azure Active Directory (AAD); pašlaik vienmēr AAD</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-279">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority\_type** – Consumer / Microsoft Service Agreement (MSA) vs organizational / Azure Active Directory (AAD); currently always AAD</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-280">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority\_validation\_status** — norāda, vai autentifikācija tika pabeigta pakalpojuma pusē</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-280">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_authority\_validation\_status** – Tells whether authentication completed on the service-side</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-281">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_broker\_app** — norāda, vai ADAL autentifikācijai izmantoja starpnieku</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-281">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_broker\_app** - Tells whether ADAL used a broker for authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-282">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_broker\_app\_used** — norāda starpnieka nosaukumu (piemēram, Windows kontu pārvaldība)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-282">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_broker\_app\_used** – Tells the name of the broker (e.g., Windows Account Management)</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-284">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count** — kešatmiņas notikumu skaits, ko ADAL veica, izgūstot marķieri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-284">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count** - Number of cache events ADAL performed while retrieving token</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-285">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_max** — ja šis signāls tiek apkopots, maksimālais jebkura apkopotā notikuma kešatmiņas notikumu skaits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-285">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_max** - If this signal is aggregated, max cache events of any one of the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-286">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_min** — ja šis signāls tiek apkopots, minimālais jebkura apkopotā notikuma kešatmiņas notikumu skaits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-286">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_min** - If this signal is aggregated, min cache events of any one of the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-287">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_sum** — ja šis signāls tiek apkopots, visu apkopoto notikumu kešatmiņas notikumu summa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-287">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_event\_count\_sum** - If this signal is aggregated, sum of the cache events of all the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-288">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_count** — cik reižu API lasīja no diska kešatmiņas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-288">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_count** - How many times the API read from the disk cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-289">Spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena lasīšana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-289">Present if there was at least one read.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-290">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_error\_count** — cik reižu diska kešatmiņas lasīšana neizdevās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-290">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_error\_count** - How many times the disk cache read failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-291">Ir spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena kļūme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-291">Is present if there was at least one failure.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-292">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_last\_error** — ADAL kļūdas kods.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-292">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_read\_last\_error** - ADAL error code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-293">Spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena lasīšanas kļūme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-293">Present if there was at least one read failure.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-296">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_count** — cik reižu API rakstīja diska kešatmiņā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-296">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_count** - How many times the API wrote to the disk cache.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-297">Spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena rakstīšana.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-297">Present if there was at least one write.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-298">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_error\_count** — cik reižu diska kešatmiņas rakstīšana neizdevās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-298">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_error\_count** - How many times the disk cache-write failed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-299">Spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena kļūme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-299">Present if there was at least one failure.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-300">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_last\_error** — ADAL kļūdas kods.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-300">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_cache\_write\_last\_error** - ADAL error code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-301">Spēkā, ja ir bijusi vismaz viena rakstīšanas kļūme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-301">Present if there was at least one write failure.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-305">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_extended\_expires\_on\_setting** — patiess/aplams norāda, vai marķierim ir pagarināts kalpošanas laiks.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-305">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_extended\_expires\_on\_setting** - True/false telling if the token has an extended lifetime.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-307">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_http\_event\_count\_max** — ja šis signāls ir apkopots, maksimālais HTTP izsaukumu skaits, ko ADAL veic jebkuram apkopotajam notikumam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-307">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_http\_event\_count\_max** - If this signal is aggregated, max HTTP calls made by ADAL of any aggregated event.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-312">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_logging\_pii\_enabled** — patiess/aplams norāda, vai ADAL pilnās reģistrēšanas režīms ir iespējots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-312">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_logging\_pii\_enabled** - True/false telling if ADAL full logging mode is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-313">Šie dati tiek reģistrēti tikai lokāli, netiek raidīti telemetrijā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-313">This data is only logged locally, not emitted in telemetry.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-314">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_oauth\_error\_code** — OAuth protokola kļūdas kods, ko atgrieza pakalpojums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-314">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_oauth\_error\_code** – OAuth protocol error code returned by the service.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-315">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_prompt\_behavior** — pieteikšanās vai nekāds HTTP parametrs tiek nodots pakalpojumam, lai norādītu, vai var rādīt lietotāja interfeisu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-315">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_prompt\_behavior** - log-in or none HTTP parameter passed to service to specify if user interface can be shown.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-317">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_code** — HTTP atbildes kods no pakalpojuma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-317">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_code** - HTTP response code from the service.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-318">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time** — cik ilgi pakalpojums atgrieza ADAL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-318">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time** - How long it took service to return to ADAL.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-319">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_max** — ja signāls ir apkopots, maksimālais laiks, cik ilgi ADAL atgriezās no API kādā no apkopotajiem notikumiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-319">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_max** - If the signal is aggregated, the max time it took ADAL to return from its API among any of the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-320">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_min** — ja signāls ir apkopots, minimālais laiks, cik ilgi pakalpojums atbildēja ADAL kādā no apkopotajiem notikumiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-320">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_min** - If the signal is aggregated, the min time it took the service to respond to ADAL among any of the aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-321">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_sum** — ja signāls ir apkopots, laika summa, cik ilgi ADAL atgriezās no API visos apkopotajos notikumos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-321">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_response\_time\_sum** - If the signal is aggregated, the sum of the time it took ADAL to return from its API among all aggregated events.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-322">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_rt\_age** — atsvaidzināšanas marķiera vecums</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-322">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_rt\_age** – Age of the refresh token</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-323">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_error\_code** — servera atgrieztais kļūdas kods</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-323">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_error\_code** - Error code returned by the server</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-324">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_sub\_error\_code** — servera atgrieztais pakārtotais kļūdas kods, lai norādītu, kāpēc pieprasījums neizdevās.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-324">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_server\_sub\_error\_code** - Sub error code returned by the server to help disambiguate why the request failed.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-325">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_spe\_ring** — patiess/aplams norāda, vai lietotājs izmantoja Secure Production Enterprise iekšējo apli (tikai Microsoft darbinieki).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-325">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_spe\_ring** - True/false telling if the user was using the Secure Production Enterprise inner ring (Microsoft employees only).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-326">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_start\_time** — laiks, kad ADAL API izsaukums tika veikts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-326">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_start\_time** – Time the ADAL API call was made</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-327">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_stop\_time** — laiks, kad ADAL API izsaukums tika atgriezts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-327">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_stop\_time** - Time the ADAL API call returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-328">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_telemetry\_pii\_enabled** — patiess/aplams norāda, vai ADAL pilnās telemetrijas režīms ir iespējots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-328">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_telemetry\_pii\_enabled** - True/false telling if ADAL full telemetry mode is enabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-329">Nosaukums ir misnomer, jo PII/EUII netiek raidīts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-329">The name is a misnomer, as no PII/EUII is emitted.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-330">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_tenant\_id** — GUID, kas identificē nomnieku, kam autentificētais lietotājs pieder.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-330">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_tenant\_id** - GUID identifying the tenant that the authenticated user belongs to.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-331">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_acquisition\_from\_context** — apraksta ADAL uzvedību, ņemot vērā marķierus autentifikācijas kontekstā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-331">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_acquisition\_from\_context** - Describes the ADAL behavior based on the tokens in the authentication context.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-332">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_type** — atsvaidzināšanas marķieris (RT) vai vairāku resursu atsvaidzināšanas marķieris (MRRT).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-332">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_token\_type** – Either refresh token (RT) or multi-resource refresh token (MRRT).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-333">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_ui\_event\_count** — uzvedņu skaits, kas tiek rādītas lietotājam.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-333">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_ui\_event\_count** - Count of prompts shown to the user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-334">Var būt klusas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-334">May have been silent.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-335">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_user\_cancel** — patiess/aplams, ja lietotāja interfeisa logs tika atcelts.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-335">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_user\_cancel** - True / false if the user interface window was cancelled.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-336">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_x\_ms\_request\_id** — papildu pieprasījuma ID, ko HTTP galvenē pakalpojumam nodrošina ADAL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-336">**Microsoft\_ADAL\_x\_ms\_request\_id** – Additional request ID provided in HTTP header to service by ADAL.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-337">**Platform** — Win32/WinRT/Android/iOS/Mac</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-337">**Platform** - Win32/WinRT/Android/iOS/Mac</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-338">**Scenarioid** — GUID.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-338">**Scenarioid** – GUID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-339">Vairāki notikumi var piederēt vienam scenārijam, piemēram, scenārijs var pievienot jaunu kontu, bet pastāv vairākas uzvednes, kas rodas kā daļa no šī scenārija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-339">Multiple events may belong to a single scenario, e.g. the scenario may be adding a new account but there are multiple prompts that occur as part of that scenario.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-340">Šis ID nodrošina korelācijas iespējamību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-340">This ID enables correlation to happen.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-341">**Sessionid** — GUID, kas identificē sāknēšanas sesiju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-341">**Sessionid** - GUID identifying the boot session</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-342">**Skdver** — MATS klienta SDK versija, kas tiek izmantota, lai radītu šos datus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-342">**Skdver** - Version of MATS client SDK used to produce this data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-343">**Starttime** — laiks, kad Start\*Action MATS API tika izsaukts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-343">**Starttime** - Time at which the Start\*Action MATS API was called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-344">**Tenantid** — GUID, kas identificē nomnieku, kam autentificētais lietotājs pieder (ar ADAL nesaistītos gadījumos).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-344">**Tenantid** - GUID identifying the tenant the authenticated user belongs to (in non-ADAL cases).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-345">**Uploadid** — unikālais GUID šim notikumam, tiek izmantots dublikātu likvidēšanai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-345">**Uploadid** - Unique GUID for this event, used for de-duping</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-346">**Wamapi** — norāda, kurš WAM API ir izsaukts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-346">**Wamapi** - Identifies which WAM API is called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** — pašlaik netiek izmantots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** - Currently unused.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-348">Nākotnē sniedz WAM komponentam iespēju izsūtīt papildinformāciju par autentifikācijas notikumu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-348">In the future, allows the WAM component to dispatch additional information regarding the authentication event.</span></span>

## <a name="click-to-run-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-349">Click-to-Run notikumi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-349">Click-to-Run events</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunbootstrapper"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-350">Office.ClickToRun.Bootstrapper</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-350">Office.ClickToRun.Bootstrapper</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-351">Office iestatīšanas un krājumu dati, kas tiek apkopoti, kad lietotājs palaiž failu Office setup.exe, lai modificētu savus instalētos Office produktus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-351">Office set up and inventory data collected when the user is running Office setup.exe to modify their installed Office products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-352">Tiek izmantots, lai mērītu pilnas lietotāja uzsāktas Office instalēšanas sekmīgu izpildi/kļūmi, tostarp priekšnoteikumu pārbaudes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-352">Used to measure success / failure of a full user-initiated Office installation including pre-requisite checks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-353">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-353">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-356">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState** — daļa, kas neizdevās boostrapperbootstrapper</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-356">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_FailingState** – The part that we failed in the boostrapperbootstrapper</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-357">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_OExceptionType** — izņēmuma veids, ar kuru radās problēmas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-357">**Data\_BootStrapperStateFailure\_OExceptionType** – The type of exception we failed with</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunmachinemetadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-406">Office.ClickToRun.MachineMetadata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-406">Office.ClickToRun.MachineMetadata</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-413">**Data\_SqmMachineID** — unikālais datora ID, ko izmanto Windows SQM Data\_SusClientID- datora Office atjaunināšanas identifikators</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-413">**Data\_SqmMachineID** – Unique Machine ID used by Windows SQM Data\_SusClientID- Machine Office update identifier</span></span>

### <a name="officeclicktorunodt"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-414">Office.ClickToRun.ODT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-414">Office.ClickToRun.ODT</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1433">Tas tiek apkopots katrā sesijā, kas ziņo datora licencēšanas stāvokli un kļūdas, kas lietotājam rodas un kuru dēļ tas nevar izmantot lietojumprogrammu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1433">This is collected on every session that reports the licensing state of the machine and reports the errors that the user is seeing due to which they are not able to use the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1434">Šis notikums norāda, vai lietotāja dators ir darbspējīgs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1434">This event indicates if the user's machine is healthy or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1435">Esam iestatījuši anomāliju noteikšanu šim notikumam, lai norādītu, vai regresija izraisa neatbilstošo lietotāju uzvedību.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1435">We have anomaly detection set up for this event to indicate if a regression is causing bad user behavior.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1436">Tas ir arī kritiski svarīgi, kad tiek diagnosticētas lietotāja problēmas, kā arī sistēmas darbspējas pārraudzībai</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1436">This is also critical when diagnosing user issues and for monitoring system health</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1437">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1437">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1439">**IsSessionLicensing** — vai pašlaik strādājam koplietojamā datora aktivizācijas režīmā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1439">**IsSessionLicensing** – Whether we are currently running under shared computer activation mode or not</span></span> 

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1440">**LicenseCategory** — lietotāja izmantotās Office licences kategorija</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1440">**LicenseCategory** – Category of the office license that the user is using</span></span> 

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1441">**Licenses** — visu datorā esošo Office licenču nosaukumu saraksts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1441">**Licenses** – List of names of all the  office licenses that are present on the machine</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensinggetentitlement"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1443">Office.Licensing.GetEntitlement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1443">Office.Licensing.GetEntitlement</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1444">Mēs to apkopojam, kad lietotājs iestata ierīci un mēs izsaucam mūsu licencēšanas pakalpojumu, lai noteiktu, vai lietotājam, kas ir pieteicies, ir Office tiesības.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1444">We collect this when the user is setting up a device and we call our licensing service to detect if the logged in user has an office entitlement or not.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1445">Tādējādi tiek norādīts attiecīgā izsaukuma rezultāts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1445">This reports the result of that call.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1446">Tas ir kritiski svarīgs, lai noteiktu, vai lietotājs ir piemērotā stāvoklī un vai tam trūkst funkcionalitātes, kas tiek izmantota sistēmas darbspējai un diagnostikas mērķiem, ja lietotājs ziņo par problēmu savā datorā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1446">It is critical in detecting if the user is in a good state and missing functionality, used for system health and used for diagnostic purposes if a user reports an issue with their machine</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensingheartbeat"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1448">Office.Licensing.Heartbeat</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1448">Office.Licensing.Heartbeat</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1449">Katrā sesijā pārbaudām, vai ir pagājušas 72 stundas kopš pēdējās licences atjaunošanas, un mēģinām pagarināt pašreizējās licences derīguma termiņu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1449">On every session we check if 72 hours have passed since the last license renewal and try to extend the expiry of the current license.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1450">Šis notikums ziņo par izsaukuma, ko veicam, lai nodrošinātu, ka varam pagarināt licences derīguma termiņu un uzturēt lietotāja Office instalācijas funkcionalitāti, sekmīgu izpildi vai kļūmi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1450">This event reports the success or failure of the call that we make to ensure we can extend the expiry of the license and keep the user's office installation functional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1451">Tas ir kritiski svarīgi, lai diagnosticētu ar abonementu saistītas problēmas un pakalpojumu problēmas lietotājam, kā arī ir kritiski svarīgi, lai noteiktu regresiju jau aktivizēto abonementu lietotājiem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1451">It is critical in diagnosing subscription related issues and service issues for the user and is critical in detecting regressions for already activated subscription users.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1452">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1452">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1500">**Office.Licensing.NextUserLicensingEligible —** šis signāls mums norāda, vai lietotājs ir kvalificēts pāriet uz mūsu jauno licencēšanas steku.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1500">**Office.Licensing.NextUserLicensingEligible -** This signal tells us if a user is qualified to move to our new licensing stack.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1501">Tas ir kritiski svarīgi, lai kvantificētu ietekmi uz esošajiem lietotājiem, kamēr ieviešam mūsu jauno licencēšanas steku un nodrošinām, ka lietotājiem nezūd funkcionalitāte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1501">This is critical to quantify the impact on existing users as we roll out our new licensing stack and make sure that users are not losing functionality</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1569">**UninstallProduct** — norāda, vai vecais produkts konvertēšanas ietvaros tiks atinstalēts</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1569">**UninstallProduct** – Indicates whether the old product will be uninstalled as part of the conversion</span></span>

### <a name="officelicensingusegracekey"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1570">Office.Licensing.UseGraceKey</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1570">Office.Licensing.UseGraceKey</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1571">Ja kāda iemesla dēļ nevaram lietotāju licencēt, instalējam pagarinājuma atslēgu un izsūtām signālu, kas to paziņo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1571">For some reason if we are unable to license the user, we install a grace key and send out this signal that signifies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1572">Tas ir kritiski svarīgs, lai noteiktu, vai lietotājs ir piemērotā stāvoklī un vai tam trūkst funkcionalitātes, kas tiek izmantota sistēmas darbspējai un diagnostikas mērķiem, ja lietotājs ziņo par problēmu savā datorā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1572">It is critical in detecting if the user is in a good state and missing functionality, used for system health and used for diagnostic purposes if a user reports an issue with their machine</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1573">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1573">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1574">**OpportunisticTokenRenewalAttempted** — norāda, vai mēģinājām oportūnistisku atjaunošanu lietotājam koplietojamā datora aktivizācijas režīmā</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1574">**OpportunisticTokenRenewalAttempted** – Indicates if we attempted an opportunistic renewal for the user in shared computer activation mode</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-1575">**ReArmResult** — norāda instalētās atslēgas atkārtotu aktivizēšanu, kas var pagarināt pašreizējās licences derīgumu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-1575">**ReArmResult** – Indicates the result of rearming the installed key which can extend the expiry of the current license</span></span>

### <a name="officesystemuserchangeddiagnosticlevel"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2090">Office.System.UserChangedDiagnosticLevel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2090">Office.System.UserChangedDiagnosticLevel</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2366">**Tag9Percent —** tag9 izmantotā procentuālā rindas daļa</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2366">**Tag9Percent -** Percentage of queue used by tag9</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetryvolumetrackingdata"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2367">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2367">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2368">Notikumu apjoma izsekošanas metrika telemetrijas notikumiem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2368">Event volume tracking metrics for telemetry events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2369">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2369">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2370">**EventThreshold** — maksimālais viena notikuma instanču skaits, ko var nosūtīt laika periodā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2370">**EventThreshold** - The maximum number of instances of a single event that can be sent in a window of time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2371">**HighestEventCount** — lielākais viena notikuma instanču skaits, kas nosūtīts šajā periodā.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2371">**HighestEventCount** - The highest number of instances of a single event sent this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2372">**HighestEventName** — notikuma ar vislielāko instanču skaitu šajā periodā nosaukums.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2372">**HighestEventName** - The name of the event with the highest number of instances in this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2373">**TimeWindowInSeconds** — perioda ilgums sekundēs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2373">**TimeWindowInSeconds** - The duration of the window in seconds.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2374">**TotalEvents** — kopējais periodā nosūtītais notikumu skaits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2374">**TotalEvents** - The total number of events sent during the window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2375">**UniqueEvents** — periodā nosūtīto unikālo notikumu skaits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2375">**UniqueEvents** - The number of unique events sent during a window.</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetrywritepayloadstodisk"></a><span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2376">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2376">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2377">Verificē, vai noteiktas mantotā konveijera daļas darbojas platformās, kas to joprojām izmanto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2377">Verifies certain parts of legacy pipeline are working on platforms that still use it.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2378">Tiek apkopoti tālāk norādītie lauki.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2378">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="bb4bf-2379">**DetachedDuration** — atvienošanas ilgums mikrosekundēs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bb4bf-2379">**DetachedDuration** - Detached duration in microseconds</span></span>
